</w:r><w:bookmarkStart w:id="3" w:name="2et92p0"/><w:bookmarkEnd w:id="3"/><w:r><w:rPr><w:b w:val="0"/></w:rPr><w:t xml:space="preserve">Furniture manufacturer, Furniture business, E-commerce website, Automated 
</w:r><w:r w:rsidR="000C4BFC"><w:tab/></w:r><w:r w:rsidR="00996B47"><w:tab/></w:r><w:r><w:rPr><w:b w:val="0"/></w:rPr><w:t>Inventory, CMS
The "
DesignXcel
" project addresses the challenges faced by 
Design Excellence Home and Office System Compa
ny
, a 
furniture manufacturing business
, in 
e-commerce website and inventory
 through a manual 
inventory
 system
 as well as the absence of an e-commerce website
. This traditional approach is prone to errors, slow processing, and limited customer convenience, often leading to dissatisfaction and operational inefficiencies. The proposed solution is a web-base
d e-commerce and inventory management with content management system
 designed to streamline the entire
 purchasing
 process, enhance 
inventorying
, and offer customers a 
better 
experience. 
A key feature of the platform is its user-friendly interface and content management system. Customers benefit from an intuitive user-friendly experience, while administrators gain access to an accessible platform with the ability to change the visual of the website. Additional modules for content management, live chat, billing, and inventory tracking to enhance the platform's functionality

INTRODUCTION
Project Context 
Businesses are switching to digital solutions to increase productivity, improve customer experience, and obtain a competitive edge, which has resulted in substantial changes in the furniture sector. Businesses who don't follow the newest trends in this fast-paced industry run the danger of losing clients to rivals that provide smooth web-based experiences. A number of obstacles impede the expansion and operational effectiveness of Design Excellence, a
 home and office
 furniture firm.
One of the most significant issues encountered by Design Excellence Home & Office System Co. is its outdated website. The current website was built using Wix, 
a
 accessible
 website-building 
but
 does not fully meet the company’s specific needs. The website lacks a well-organized and user-friendly layout, especially when accessed on smartphones, making it less accessible and u
nu
sable for potential customers. Additionally, the company is paying for the platform but has limited control over editing and updating its content, leading to outdated product descriptions and inaccurate information. This lack of control negatively impacts customer trust and the company’s credibility.
The company's inventory management is another significant problem. At the moment, Design Excellence uses Microsoft Excel to manage supply, keep an eye on stock levels, and manage the procurement process. This manual method is ineffective for real-time tracking, sluggish, and prone to mistakes. The lack of an automated system leads to order fulfilment bottlenecks, which raises the possibility of raw material mishandling, delays, and stock shortages. Productivity and customer satisfaction are directly impacted by these operational inefficiencies.
The proponents
 
will be
 creating DesignXcel, an integrated web-based solution made to specifically fulfill the requirements of Design Excellence, in order to overcome these issues. In addition to improving the company's online visibility, this system will combine essential business functions to optimize operations. All users will have the best possible experience thanks to the new platform's
 
CMS (
Content Management System)
. Consumers will find it easy to choose from a variety of furniture selections, 
color selections
, and make 
quotations
.
DesignXcel will also include an innovative inventory management system that will automate stock tracking and allow for real-time monitoring. Order fulfilment and procurement procedures will be enhanced and mistakes will be decreased as a result. A committed staff member will be on hand to answer questions in real time, guaranteeing seamless communication and increased client involvement in order to improve customer service. To make it simpler for companies to buy office furniture in bulk.
An
 
Order Tracker 
that lets users track their purchases and see projected delivery times will be included in DesignXcel for more transparency. In order to provide flexibility, the platform will accept a number of payment options, such as cash
 on-delivery
, 
e-wallet
s
, and bank transfers.
In addition 
to overcoming its current obstacles, Design Excellence will enhance customer happiness, operational effectiveness, and business expansion by putting DesignXcel into practice. By using contemporary digital technologies, the business will be positioned to compete in the office furniture sector, guaranteeing its viability and success in the changing market.
Purpose and Description of the 
Project
The goal of this project is to develop DesignXcel, a web-based system designed to enhance the online presence and operational efficiency of Design Excellence. This system will improve website functionality, simplify inventory management, and enhance customer service by providing real-time communication and order tracking.
What makes this project unique is its combination of an interactive
 content management system
 
and an automated inventory management system. Additionally, the inclusion of a dedicated support feature ensures that customer inquiries are addressed promptly, leading to a smoother and more satisfying shopping experience.
Objectives of the Study
General Objective
The objective of this study is to design and develop DesignXcel, a fully functional web-based system aimed at enhancing the digital presence of Design Excellence. The system seeks to provide a user-friendly, mobile-responsive, and efficient online platform that improves product visibility, customer engagement,
 as well as automate the inventory management, make a CMS feature to make website editing easier without prior technical expertise
 and overall business operations.
Specific Objective
Specifically, this
 study aims to:
Develop a user-friendly and mobile-responsive 
e-commerce 
website that provides accurate and up-to-date product listings to ensure a seamless browsing and shopping experience for customers.
Implement an automated inventory management system that enables real-time stock monitoring, minimizes errors, and streamlines procurement and order fulfillment processes.
Include a content management system to the system 
for managing product listings, updating descriptions, and adjusting prices. 
An e
asy-to-use interface for modifying website content without needing technical expertise.
Integrate real-time communication features that allow customers to interact directly with customer service representatives and receive transparent updates on order progress
.
Scope and Limitations of the Study
Scope of the project:
The purpose of this study is to design and develop DesignXcel, a web-based system to enhance the digital presence and operational efficiency of Design Excellence. The target users of the system 
are Design Excellence employees, individual customers looking to purchase office furniture, and
 business customers seeking bulk orders. The study will focus on the period from development to deployment, testing, and evaluation of the system's impact on business operations.
The features of the proposed system include:
E-commerce w
ebsite
Product variant and color selections showcase: The ability of the system to view the in-depth details and select product variants and colors.
Customer Inquiry and 
Real-Time
 
Support: 
A real-time communication feature for customer support, allowing customers to interact with a dedicated representative.
Payment Options: 
The system only accepts
 
e-wallet
s
 as of now.
Bulk Orders:
 
Allows customers to purchase large quantities of products in a single transaction.
Inventory
 Management
</w:r></w:p><w:p w14:paraId="7FF1BCB1" w14:textId="66726F80" w:rsidR="000908CA" w:rsidRPr="000908CA" w:rsidRDefault="000908CA" w:rsidP="000908CA"><w:pPr><w:pStyle w:val="ListParagraph"/><w:numPr><w:ilvl w:val="0"/><w:numId w:val="1"/></w:numPr><w:spacing w:line="360" w:lineRule="auto"/><w:jc w:val="both"/><w:rPr><w:b w:val="0"/><w:bCs/><w:lang w:val="en-US"/></w:rPr></w:pPr><w:r w:rsidRPr="001608F6"><w:rPr><w:b w:val="0"/><w:bCs/></w:rPr><w:t>Content Management System (CMS):
 
Admin dashboard for updating product details and uploading visuals through an easy-to-use interface.
</w:r></w:p><w:p w14:paraId="217C5296" w14:textId="64A5D41F" w:rsidR="00AF4E79" w:rsidRDefault="00AF4E79" w:rsidP="00AF4E79"><w:pPr><w:pStyle w:val="ListParagraph"/><w:numPr><w:ilvl w:val="0"/><w:numId w:val="1"/></w:numPr><w:spacing w:line="360" w:lineRule="auto"/><w:jc w:val="both"/><w:rPr><w:b w:val="0"/><w:bCs/></w:rPr></w:pPr><w:r w:rsidRPr="0016353C"><w:rPr><w:b w:val="0"/></w:rPr><w:t xml:space="preserve">Automated Inventory Management System: 
An automated inventory management system to enable real-time tracking of stock levels and order fulfilment.
User Role Management: Access control for different system users (e.g., 
inventory manager, transaction manager, user manager
).
Activity logs: Ability to check user activities like changes in the inventory and who changed the inventory.
Sales report
: 
Summarizes transactions and sales performance over specific periods to help the company track trends and revenue.
Limitations
:
 
Internet-dependent platform
:
 The system requires continuous and stable internet connectivity for users and administrators to access product listings, place orders, manage inventory, or update the CMS. Any interruption in connection prevents system usage.
Mobile application not supported
: DesignXcel is a responsive web application and does not include a native mobile app; functionality and layout may vary by browser and device.
Manual verification of newly added content
: 
Uploaded products, images, and promotional content must still be manually reviewed and approved by an administrator before going live, which may delay publishing.
Single-language interface
: 
All system text, product information, and interface elements are presented only in English. Support for additional languages or localization is not available.
Single-currency payment processing
: 
The platform only supports Philippine Peso (PHP) for product purchases. Users from other regions cannot view or pay using alternative currencies.
Site-visit project handling: Large or custom orders that necessitate on-site measurements and formal contracts fall outside the scope of the online system and must be managed offline.
External payment gateway dependency: Payment processing relies on third-party digital wallet providers. Any downtime, delays, or issues from these providers directly affect the system's checkout process.
REVIEW OF RELATED LITERATURE/SYSTEMS
Review of Related Literature
Local
 
Literature
According to RichestPH
 (
2023), the digital transformation journey in the Philippines showcases a progressive trend across various industries, highlighting both challenges and success stories. Companies such as Globe Telecom, Ayala Corporation, Jollibee, BPI, and San Miguel Corporation serve as prime examples of how integrating technology can enhance efficiency and improve customer experiences. These enterprises have demonstrated that innovation, collaboration, and continuous learning are essential for staying competitive in a rapidly evolving digital landscape. As more businesses in the Philippines acknowledge the necessity of digital adaptation, their ability to navigate and implement technological advancements will determine their resilience and long-term success in an increasingly digital economy.
According to STOFLY 
(
2024), technology has significantly influenced various aspects of life, including the custom furniture industry in the Philippines. Traditionally, Filipino furniture craftsmanship has been deeply rooted in artistry, patience, and a strong connection to nature. However, with the integration of modern digital tools, the industry is undergoing a transformation that blends old-world elegance with modern innovation. The adoption of technology in custom furniture design has allowed businesses to enhance precision, streamline production, and cater to a more dynamic market. This shift not only preserves traditional craftsmanship but also ensures that Filipino furniture makers remain competitive in an increasingly digital world.
According to RichestPH
 (
2022), the COVID-19 pandemic accelerated digital transformation among Filipino businesses, pushing them to adopt new technologies and operational models to mitigate the effects of restrictions. Companies rapidly transitioned to online commerce, integrated collaboration tools, and enhanced customer engagement strategies to maintain business continuity. This shift not only helped businesses survive during the crisis but also prepared them for long-term resilience in an increasingly digital economy. The adoption of digital solutions has become a crucial factor in staying competitive, especially in industries such as retail and manufacturing, where customer experience and operational efficiency are key to sustaining growth.
According to Apilado et 
al.
 
(
2022
)
, the furniture industry in Gulod, Labac, Batangas City faced various challenges during the pandemic era, including supply chain disruptions, late deliveries, and material shortages. Through interviews with a local factory owner, the study highlighted the difficulties in sourcing high-quality wood such as Nara and the importance of workforce allocation in furniture production. The study utilized a descriptive research design, incorporating case studies and observations to analyze operational processes in the furniture and sash manufacturing sector. Findings revealed that local manufacturers rely on a mix of imported and locally sourced materials, with varying degrees of availability. The study emphasized the importance of efficient inventory and resource management in maintaining production flow and meeting customer demands.
According to 
U
NIVIO 
(
2024
)
, effective product base organization and system integration are crucial for scaling product offerings and launching an online marketplace. The study highlights the role of Pimcore’s integration with Baselinker in
 
enabling direct sales in foreign markets, allowing businesses to expand efficiently. Additionally, the Unilinker integration platform provided enhanced performance and flexibility, ensuring seamless data management across different sales channels. The study emphasizes the importance of selecting appropriate 
technological
 solutions to optimize digital transformation efforts. With the support 
of the Univio team, businesses were able to implement these technologies successfully, demonstrating the significance of strategic digital system adoption in modern e-commerce and inventory management.
According to Yambao et
.
 al
.
 
(
2022
)
, the adoption of augmented reality (AR) technology in the furniture industry significantly enhances customer experience by providing real-time status updates and interactive product previews. Their study evaluated a mobile application using the ISO 25010 standards, where it was deemed highly acceptable. The research further emphasized that AR technology allows customers to visualize made-to-order furniture within their intended space, improving decision-
making,
 and purchase satisfaction. Additionally, the study suggested that integrating emerging technologies like mixed reality could further refine 
customer
 experience and extend applicability to other industries requiring product visualization.
According to Richtek 
(
2025), computerized inventory systems play a crucial role in automating the inventory management process for businesses in the Philippines. These systems provide essential features such as inventory control, management, tracking, and optimization, which significantly enhance operational efficiency. The integration of such digital solutions enables businesses to streamline their processes, minimize errors, and ensure real-time monitoring of stock levels. By utilizing computerized inventory systems, businesses can effectively respond to market demands, reduce operational bottlenecks, and maintain accurate records of stock movements. The study highlights that adopting automated inventory management solutions is vital for achieving a competitive advantage, as it allows businesses to swiftly adapt to market fluctuations and improve overall productivity.
According to DynamIQ 
(
2024), Running a business requires hard work, but as operations grow, managing inventory can become complex. Fortunately, technology offers a solution through Inventory Management Systems (IMS), like SAP Business One from DynamIQ, a Gold Partner in the Philippines. This software 
streamlines inventory processes, 
can save 
time and 
reduce
 errors for businesses of all sizes by centralizing stock, orders, and deliveries. Key benefits include real-time inventory tracking, which enhances visibility and prevents stockouts; reduced human error through automation; streamlined order fulfilment for faster processing; and data-driven decision-making that identifies trends and optimizes purchasing.
According to DynamIQ 
(
2024), managing inventory becomes increasingly complex as a business grows, making technological solutions essential. The study highlights the role of Inventory Management Systems (IMS), such as SAP Business One, in streamlining inventory processes for businesses in the Philippines. As a Gold Partner of SAP, DynamIQ emphasizes how this system centralizes stock, orders, and deliveries, improving overall efficiency. The key advantages of IMS include real-time inventory tracking, which enhances visibility and prevents stock shortages, as well as automation features that minimize human errors. Additionally, the system facilitates streamlined order fulfilment, leading to faster processing and improved customer satisfaction. Through data-driven decision-making, businesses can analyze trends and optimize procurement, ensuring operational effectiveness. The study underscores the importance of digital transformation in inventory management, aligning with the need for businesses to adopt modern solutions to stay competitive in the evolving market.
According to Nugrahani
 (
2025), inventory management software is a comprehensive system designed to track, organize, and oversee inventory in real time. It automates processes such as monitoring stock levels, orders, sales, and deliveries, reducing human errors and ensuring operational efficiency. Poor inventory management can lead to significant financial losses, as evidenced by the $132 billion lost in retail shrink due to theft, errors, and fraud in 2025. By integrating inventory management software, businesses can avoid common issues like stockouts, overstocking, and manual inaccuracies, allowing them to streamline their operations effectively.
Furthermore, inventory management software enhances supply chain efficiency by providing real-time visibility into stock levels and enabling data-driven decision-making. Businesses utilizing this technology experience increased productivity, improved space utilization, and optimized stock efficiency. Studies show that integrating order processing within inventory management software can lead to a 25% rise in productivity, a 20% enhancement in space usage, and a 30% increase in stock accuracy. The two main types of inventory systems, periodic and perpetual, play essential roles in stock management, with perpetual systems offering real-time tracking to optimize supply chain processes. By adopting such solutions, companies can significantly improve operational effectiveness, reduce costs, and maintain better control over their inventory.
According to Arrafi 
(
2024), effective inventory management is essential for business success, particularly in the dynamic Philippine market. Ensuring that businesses maintain the right stock levels helps prevent lost sales and reduces the risk of overstocking, which can lead to increased storage costs and potential product wastage. Proper inventory management enhances profitability by optimizing operational efficiency, freeing up capital for reinvestment in key areas such as marketing, product development, and business expansion. Additionally, maintaining an organized inventory system fosters customer trust, leading to improved satisfaction and loyalty. When businesses consistently have products available, customers are more likely to return and recommend their services. Implementing an efficient inventory management system not only strengthens overall business performance but also contributes to long-term sustainability in competitive industries.
According to Zosa (2024), the Cebu furniture industry has a long history of globalization, dating back to the 1950s when it became a dominant exporter of rattan furniture. By partnering with international buyers, Cebu was able to establish a strong presence in the global market. However, beginning in the 1980s, the industry experienced a steady decline as countries such as Malaysia, China, and 
Vietnam emerged as key players, displacing Cebu’s market share. Despite this decline, the Cebu furniture industry remains a vital part of the local economy, continuing to be one of the province’s top export earners. The industry's ability to adapt and sustain itself highlights the importance of innovation and modernization in maintaining competitiveness in the global furniture market. Implementing digital transformation strategies, such as automated inventory management and e-commerce integration, could further enhance Cebu’s furniture sector by improving efficiency and expanding market reach.

According to Harper
 (
2023), IKEA’s digital transformation, led by Barbara Martin Coppola, aimed to modernize the company while preserving its core values, resulting in significant operational and cultural changes. Within three years, IKEA tripled its e-commerce sales and transformed its physical stores into fulfilment centers, requiring a complete overhaul of its supply chain, store layouts, and logistics. The shift to online retail also meant adapting to a dual-speed operation, as physical stores had fixed hours while online platforms operated 24/7. By leveraging algorithms, IKEA optimized its logistics to ensure cost-effective deliveries from either distribution centers or retail stores. This transformation highlights the crucial role of digitalization in enhancing customer experience, improving supply chain efficiency, and maintaining competitiveness in the evolving furniture industry.

According to Zeihar et al, 
(
2023), numerous studies have examined and substantiated the impact of digital transformation, demonstrating its ability to create new value propositions across various industries. While meta-studies have developed classifications and frameworks to consolidate existing knowledge, there remains a gap in research that specifically integrates industry-focused insights, particularly in the furniture sector. In response to this, Zeihar et al. conducted a systematic literature search on digital transformation within the furniture industry, analyzing insights from 85 scholarly papers. Their study proposed a theory-driven framework with five key focal areas: sources of disruption, strategic responses, value creation transformation, technical applications, and obstacles to implementation. By structuring and synthesizing existing research using this framework, the study provided a comprehensive understanding of digital 
transformation in the furniture industry and identified potential directions for future research.
Hence, 
digital transformation in the furniture industry has been significantly influenced by emerging 
technologies (Rame et al, 2023). 
The study conducted a systematic literature review using recent publications from ScienceDirect and Scopus databases to analyze various digital innovations adopted by furniture businesses to enhance efficiency, sustainability, and competitiveness. The research highlights the role of automation, robotics, augmented reality, and the Internet of Things (IoT) in optimizing furniture production processes, minimizing waste, and improving overall profitability. Additionally, it discusses sustainable and socially responsible approaches such as green supply chain management, life cycle assessment, and ergonomic design solutions. The findings emphasize the importance of developing a comprehensive digital transformation strategy that integrates advanced technologies, fosters innovative business models, and upholds sustainability and ethical standards within the industry.

Synthesis
The increasing shift toward digital transformation across industries underscores its vital role in enhancing efficiency and maintaining competitiveness. In the Philippines, businesses ranging from large corporations to small enterprises have leveraged technology to streamline processes, improve customer interactions, and stay responsive to market trends. Likewise, the furniture sector has embraced digital innovations to balance traditional craftsmanship with modern production methods. The adoption of inventory management systems, cloud-based platforms, and automation has enabled businesses to minimize errors, monitor stock levels in real time, and make data-driven decisions, ensuring long-term success in an evolving digital landscape.
Globally, companies like IKEA have demonstrated how digital transformation can revolutionize operations by optimizing logistics, integrating online and offline retail, and utilizing data analytics to enhance customer experiences. Research in the furniture industry highlights the significance of omnichannel strategies, automation, and efficient inventory management in staying competitive. The use of ERP systems, AI-powered solutions, and digital marketplaces has transformed business operations, allowing companies to expand and adapt efficiently. These insights reinforce that adopting digital solutions is no longer a choice but a critical factor in achieving sustainability and growth in today’s dynamic global market

Software
 
Requirements
Calendar of Activities
Activities commenced after the orientation for capstone 1 was conducted on January 30, 2025, which is referred to as week 1. Followed by group creations and the assignment of a thesis adviser on February 7, 2025.
<w:t>Brainstorming
The proponents had a meeting to figure out the areas to improve the whole construction of the system. It helps to generate a wide range of creative ideas and opportunities to make the platform successful.
<w:t>Proposal Approval
Presenting a thoroughly thought-out and polished project idea to the faculty for assessment was a step in the proposal approval procedure. The group made sure the initiative complied with industry and academic standards by outlining its goals, parameters, and possible effects. The proposals were presented, leading to the panel approving DesignXcel as the capstone project
<w:t>Data Gathering
By implementing a comprehensive data gathering strategy, DesignXcel can continually improve its platform, empower Furniture Manufacturing business, and improve market visibility by using the proponents created website/project.
<w:t>Interview
T
he proponents conducted multiple interviews with the client to figure out the existing problem of the company and had an agreement on how the researchers 
would
 fix the said problems.
<w:t>Planning
The proponents had a meeting to plan the establishment for 
DesignXcel
's functionalities. This ensures everyone on the research team is on the same page, avoiding any wasted effort. It allows to build 
DesignXcel
 efficiently, effectively, and with a clear vision in mind, ultimately delivering a valuable and impactful system.
<w:t>Designing
After gathering information from Design Excellence, a 
proposal for
 design of the system is created that includes the vital parts of the system for the client to have an idea on how the outcome will look like.
</w:r><w:r><w:rPr><w:rFonts w:cs="Times New Roman"/></w:rPr><w:t>System Development
The proponents focused on system development by setting up the development environment, designing the database, and implementing both front-end and back-end components. Key modules such as user management, product listings, and core functionalities were developed and integrated. Internal testing was conducted to ensure basic functionality and system stability, with regular coordination among group members and the thesis adviser to align progress with project goals. By the end of this phase, a working prototype with most core features was completed.
Gantt Chart of Activities
Legend:
 
Yellow
 = Ongoing, 
Blue
 = Complete, 
Red
 = Incomplete

4
. Gantt Chart
Hardware
Laptop – A personal laptop, equipped with a Intel core i3-1005G1 CPU, and 8gb of RAM, was used to develop the project.
Software
Database Management – 
The developers
 used Node.js to 
connect
 
our
 Microsoft SQL or MSSQL database so that we may access and save some of the data we need in our system. Our database will house the data administrators, users, and products.
Visual Studio Code – Visual Studio Code was used to develop the system. For creating the features. Using EJS, JavaScript, and lastly CSS.
Requirements Analysis
To create an inventory management system along with a website for Design Excellence Home and Office System Company, it is important to focus on the needs of both the staff and customers. The company staff will use the system as the main tool for organizing their inventory, while customers will be able to use the website to view the furniture gallery, access detailed product information, use customer chat support, and make inquiries—making the process quicker and more convenient.  
The versatility of the website will be increased as the administrator will be able to choose which furniture is shown. Customizing the website won't require technical expertise thanks to the CMS functionality. This include maintaining product listings, revising product descriptions, and modifying product costs. In the end, the system will enhance overall service quality and simplify inventory management.

Design of Software, System, Product, and/or Processes
The design of the web-based event management system for Design Excellence Home and Office System Company will follow a structured development process, ensuring the solution is user-friendly, and adheres to industry standards. This section outlines the critical components of the system design, detailing how the platform will operate, and the methodologies applied to achieve the project goals. 
The website’s system design is made for
 an e-commerce website and inventory management
. React.JS, EJS, J
ava
S
cript
, CSS, and MSSQL
 
are one of the important tools used to build this website. The event management system 
improves
 inventorying by using an automatic inventory system, removing the use for multiple digital organizers for their inventory like quickbooks and excel. 
The 
website 
also 
has a domain for easy user access
 and accessibility
.
Figure
 
1
. 
Data flow diagram
The Data Flow Diagram (DFD) illustrates how data moves between customers, administrative employees, and various processes within the system. Customers can browse products freely but must log in or register before placing an order. The system manages user credentials and profile data through the Account Management process and provides real-time assistance via Chat Support with automated FAQs. Once logged in, customers can add products to their cart, proceed to checkout, and update personal information. Completed orders are stored in the Order Management process, where customers can track, cancel, or confirm receipt of orders and later submit product reviews or ratings. 
On the administrative side, employees handle Product and Inventory Management, including adding, editing, and deactivating products, managing raw materials, and ensuring stock levels reflect customer activity. The Order Management process allows administrators to monitor and update order statuses, while the Content Management System (CMS) enables customization of website design, automated responses, and review moderation. All actions performed by employees are recorded in the Activity Logs, ensuring transparency and accountability within the system’s operations.
Figure
 
2
. 
Work Breakdown Structure (WBS)
This work breakdown structure (WBS) outlines the core components of DesignXcel, a web-based e-commerce and inventory management system integrated with a content management system for Design Excellence Home and Office System Company. The system is divided into four main modules: Chat Support, which enables automated responses and real-time messaging; Customer Interface, which manages user access, product browsing, inquiries, project galleries, shopping cart, and policies; Admin Interface, which provides administrative tools for dashboard monitoring, sales reporting, inventory control, transaction management, user administration, content management, and activity logs; and Ordering, which handles customer details and purchase histories. Together, these components ensure efficient customer interaction, streamlined operations, and effective content and inventory management.
Development
The development of DesignXcel utilized the Waterfall Model as its software development methodology. This approach was chosen because it follows a structured and sequential process where each phase of the project is completed before moving on to the next. Through this model, the team was able to maintain clear documentation, defined goals, and an organized flow of work throughout the development process. It was found to be appropriate for the DesignXcel project since the system requirements were already well defined at the start, and only minimal changes were anticipated during implementation. The Waterfall method allowed the researchers to concentrate on creating a stable and fully functional platform that combines e-commerce features, automated inventory management, and a content management system. This ensured that all project objectives were achieved with accuracy, efficiency, and consistency.
For the design of the software system for Design Excellence Home and Office System Company, the approach must follow the standard practices to ensure a robust, scalable, and user-friendly 
e-commerce 
website and inventory management system. 
The development phase is divided into three core activities
:
Database Creation & Population –
 
The team designs the database structure, sets relationships, and fills it with test data to ensure efficient and reliable storage.
Back-End Coding/Programming 
–
 
Server-side logic, APIs, and integrations are coded with proper security and validation to ensure smooth system performance.
Front-End Development 
–
 
The user interface is designed and built for responsiveness, interactivity, and accessibility across devices.
RESULTS AND DISCUSSION
Testing
The proponents evaluated the system based on software development standards to ensure it met the required functionality, availability, accessibility, and user satisfaction. Test cases were used to verify system integrity and confirm that each feature performed as intended. A four-point Likert scale survey was also conducted to gather user feedback on the system’s performance, with results analyzed through mean and standard deviation to assess overall effectiveness and user acceptance.
This is a sample of how the proponents conducted the test cases. The example shown, “TestCase_ChatSupport,” demonstrates how the chat support feature was tested to ensure its functions and design worked as intended
.

. 
Text Case Sample
Description of Prototype
To run the prototype system, the system must have at least 
a minimum
 of 
4
GB of RAM. The design 
for the e-commerce website consists of products, 
galleries
, testimonials, chat support, product 
carts,
 and contacts. For the inventory system, it consists of products listing, raw materials listing, transactions/orders section, manage users, chat support, 
logs,
 and content management system (CMS). 
The testing protocol has been carefully drafted, and any mistakes or changes that are needed must be made. The assessment procedure is well-written, and any mistakes or adjustments that are needed will be noted.
Implementation Plan
The implementation of the system will involve deploying a web-based platform to replace the multiple inventory system for ordering and managing products and materials. Key tasks include testing to ensure smooth functionality. Necessary resources, such as servers, web hosting, and software tools will be allocated. The system will be deployed starting with internal testing and then launching for customer use.
Implementation Results
The survey was conducted to
 5 employees and 25 customers with a total of 30 to
 evaluate the functional
lity
, 
availability
, 
accessibility
, and 
satisfaction
 regarding the 
DesignXcel
 platform. Results were analyzed using the mean and standard deviation to determine the level of agreement among respondents.
 
 Here are the results
.

<w:tcPr><w:tcW w:w="3420" w:type="dxa"/><w:vAlign w:val="center"/></w:tcPr><w:p w14:paraId="204296FB" w14:textId="5D3593D0" w:rsidR="00462338" w:rsidRPr="00BB2AE3" w:rsidRDefault="00BD59DF" w:rsidP="00462338"><w:pPr><w:rPr><w:b w:val="0"/><w:color w:val="000000"/><w:sz w:val="22"/><w:szCs w:val="20"/></w:rPr></w:pPr><w:r w:rsidRPr="00BB2AE3"><w:rPr><w:b w:val="0"/><w:bCs/><w:color w:val="000000"/><w:sz w:val="22"/><w:szCs w:val="20"/></w:rPr><w:t xml:space="preserve">Agreement but with 
consistent responses
.
Table 
7
. 
Functionality
 Survey
The assessment of the system’s functionality revealed a strong overall agreement among respondents, with mean scores ranging from 3.4 to 3.6. The statement “The tools in DesignXcel are reliable” received the highest mean score (M = 3.6, SD = 0.50), indicating that users found the system dependable and effective in performing its intended tasks. 
Likewise, “The features of DesignXcel are easy to use” earned a high rating (M = 3.5, SD = 0.49), reflecting user satisfaction with the platform’s usability and interface. Meanwhile, “The platform provides all the functions I need” had the lowest mean score (M = 3.4, SD = 0.48), suggesting that while users generally agree on its completeness, some perceive room for improvement in feature coverage. Overall, the findings demonstrate that DesignXcel’s functional aspects meet user expectations, with only minor refinements needed to enhance overall user experience.

consistent responses
.
Table 
9
. 
Availability
The evaluation of the system’s availability showed an overall agreement among respondents, with mean scores ranging from 3.3 to 3.4. The statement “The platform rarely experiences downtime or errors” received the highest mean score (M = 3.4, SD = 0.47), suggesting that users generally find DesignXcel reliable and consistently accessible. 
Meanwhile, both “DesignXcel is available whenever I need it” and “The system responds quickly when I use it” obtained similar ratings (M = 3.3, SD = 0.46), reflecting agreement that the platform performs well but with slightly varied perceptions of responsiveness and accessibility. Overall, the results indicate that the system provides stable availability, ensuring users can rely on it for continuous access with only minimal opportunities for enhancement.

 responses

Table 
1
1
. 
Accessibility
The assessment of the system’s accessibility showed generally positive feedback from respondents, with mean scores ranging from 3.2 to 3.6. The statement “The user interface is simple and easy to navigate” received the highest mean score (M = 3.6, SD = 0.49), indicating that users found the system intuitive and user-friendly. Similarly, “The text, layout, and visuals are clear and easy to understand” earned a strong rating (M = 3.5, SD = 0.50), reflecting user satisfaction with the platform’s clarity and visual organization. 
However, “The platform design is inclusive and accessible” obtained the lowest mean score (M = 3.2, SD = 0.40), suggesting that while users generally agreed on its accessibility, some believed there is room for improvement in ensuring inclusivity. Overall, the results indicate that DesignXcel performs well in accessibility, providing a clear and easy-to-navigate experience, with potential enhancements to make the system more inclusive for all users.

3
. 
Satisfaction
The assessment of user satisfaction revealed a strong overall agreement among respondents (M = 3.6, SD = 0.50). The majority of users expressed that they were satisfied with their overall experience using DesignXcel, reflecting a high level of approval toward the system’s performance and usability. Although there were slightly varied responses, the results indicate that users generally had a positive experience with the platform. Overall, the findings suggest that DesignXcel successfully meets user expectations and delivers a satisfying experience.
C
ONCLUSION
The development of DesignXcel successfully addressed the operational challenges faced by Design Excellence Home and Office System Company through the integration of a responsive e-commerce website, an automated inventory management system, and a dynamic content management system (CMS). The project achieved its objectives of enhancing the company’s digital presence, improving inventory accuracy, and streamlining customer interactions. By consolidating key business functions into a single web-based platform, the system improved efficiency, minimized manual errors, and provided a more seamless experience for both customers and administrators.
Evaluation results demonstrated that the system performed effectively in terms of functionality, availability, accessibility, and user satisfaction. Users expressed a high level of agreement that DesignXcel was reliable, responsive, and easy to navigate. The automated inventory feature ensured accurate, real-time stock monitoring, while the e-commerce component simplified product browsing and purchasing processes. Additionally, the CMS empowered administrators to manage and update content efficiently without requiring technical expertise, resulting in a platform that adapts quickly to business needs and market changes.
The implementation of DesignXcel represents a meaningful step toward digital transformation within the company. By integrating automation, user-centered design, and responsive technology, the system redefined how the business manages its operations and interacts with customers. This transformation reflects a broader shift from manual processes to intelligent, data-driven solutions, creating a more efficient and customer-focused environment. The system’s coherence between design and functionality not only enhances operational productivity but also reinforces brand credibility and customer trust through improved accessibility and reliability.
To sustain and enhance the platform’s performance, several improvements are recommended. Future development may include expanding payment integrations to 
support multiple currencies and digital wallets, implementing analytics dashboards to track business performance, and optimizing mobile responsiveness for wider device compatibility. Additionally, incorporating adaptive content features and marketing automation can further strengthen user engagement and administrative flexibility.
In conclusion, DesignXcel proved to be an effective and innovative solution that streamlined Design Excellence’s business processes, elevated customer experience, and modernized its overall operations. By merging technology, functionality, and usability into a unified platform, the system not only fulfilled its objectives but also positioned the company for long-term growth in the digital marketplace. With continuous enhancement and integration of advanced features, DesignXcel holds strong potential to serve as a sustainable and scalable model for digital transformation in the furniture and retail industries.
